</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A structured activity or form of play with defined rules and objectives.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameParticipation">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reified entity capturing the n-ary relationship of a player engaging in a specific game alongside another player.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Participation</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#participant">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Links a game participation instance to the primary player involved.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">participant</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameParticipation"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Player"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#playedGame">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Links a game participation instance to the specific game being played.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">played game</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameParticipation"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#coParticipant">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Links a game participation instance to the other player participating in the same game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">co participant</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameParticipation"/>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A structured activity or form of play with defined rules and objectives.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameParticipation">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reified entity capturing the n-ary relationship of a player engaging in a specific game alongside another player.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Participation</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reward or recognition earned by a player for completing a specific task or reaching a milestone.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AchievementType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or classification describing the nature or kind of an achievement.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or style that characterizes a game based on its gameplay, theme, or mechanics.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Genre</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Item">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An object, collectible, or entity that can be found, used, or interacted with within a game environment.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Item</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

  <!-- owl:ObjectProperty declarations -->

</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A structured activity or form of play with defined rules and objectives.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Participation</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or style that characterizes a game based on its gameplay, theme, or mechanics.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Genre</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Item">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An object, collectible, or entity that can be found, used, or interacted with within a game environment.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Item</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Ability">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A special power, skill, or effect that an item can grant or possess.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Ability</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<?xml version="1.0"?>
<rdf:RDF xml:base="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"
         xmlns:owl="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
         xmlns:rdf="http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#"
         xmlns:rdfs="http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#"
         xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#">

  <owl:Ontology rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"/>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Player">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A person who participates in a game or activity.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A structured activity or form of play with defined rules and objectives.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameParticipation">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reified entity capturing the n-ary relationship of a player engaging in a specific game alongside another player.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Participation</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reward or recognition earned by a player for completing a specific task or reaching a milestone.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AchievementType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or classification describing the nature or kind of an achievement.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or style that characterizes a game based on its gameplay, theme, or mechanics.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Genre</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Item">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An object, collectible, or entity that can be found, used, or interacted with within a game environment.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Item</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Ability">

</owl:Class>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Player">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A person who participates in a game or activity.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A structured activity or form of play with defined rules and objectives.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameParticipation">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reified entity capturing the n-ary relationship of a player engaging in a specific game alongside another player.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Participation</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reward or recognition earned by a player for completing a specific task or reaching a milestone.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AchievementType">

</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Genre</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Item">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Item</rdfs:label>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Equipment">

======================================================================
<?xml version="1.0"?>
